  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                      <strong title="Lucene Fields" class="name">Lucene Fields:</strong> 
                      <div id="customfield_12310120-val" class="value type-multicheckboxes" data-fieldtype="multicheckboxes" data-fieldtypecompletekey="com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.customfieldtypes:multicheckboxes">

              <div id="descriptionmodule" class="module toggle-wrap">
               <div id="descriptionmodule_heading" class="mod-header">
                <ul class="ops"></ul>
                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>The FST uses a single contiguous byte[] under the hood, which in java is indexed by int so we cannot grow this over Integer.MAX_VALUE. It also internally encodes references to this array as vInt.</p> 
                  <p>We could switch this to a paged byte[] and make the far larger.</p> 
                  <p>But I think this is low priority... I'm not going to work on it any time soon.</p> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div>
              </div>

src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Carlos Gonz\\u00E1lez-Cadenas\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13162156_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'03\\/Dec\\/11 15:31\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-12-03T15:31:51+0000\'\u003e03\\/Dec\\/11 15:31\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eHello Dawid:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eFirst of all, for the FSTLookup we\'re using a FST and not a FSA, that means that we\'ve replaced the NoOutputs with ByteSequenceOutputs. The reason for this is that our autocomplete system requires to get some metadata about the sentence being matched, because we do some post-match reranking of the results in order to get quality suggestions (the buckets themselves are quite big and the results are quite poor without reranking, specially for short prefixes)\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe queries we use with the FSTLookup are generated using templates. Our domain is hotels, simplifying things that means that we have K templates (i.e. an example template could be hotels + amenity + city), then we have I individuals (i.e. all the cities in the world ), and we generate queries like:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ehotels with jacuzzi in barcelona\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe output for this key contains some metadata that is useful for reranking matches or displaying the matches to the user. We encode it in as few bytes as possible, and we make sure that things that are common to many sentences are put first so that they can get compacted appropriately. The metadata in the output is the following (in order):\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e1) Display version of the sentence. The match sentence described above is normalized and transliterated to ASCII, i.e. it converts acutes to normal characters, and stuff like this. We have the \\\"display\\\" version to show the correctly formatted version to the user. We apply simple transliteration rules so that the differnece between the display and the match is not very big (i.e. , we don\'t apply stuff like pinyin transliteration for chinese).\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n2) The ID of the city (an int that will help us to later execute the query and give the right results)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n3) The \\\"score\\\" of the sentence (float, used to rerank the matches)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n4) A byte to represent the number of alternate names used in the query (i.e. \\\"barcelona\\\" is also referred as \\\"la ciudad condal\\\", if the prefix is \\\"hotels in\\\" we don\'t want to produce both matches, just the most common one. This value is used for reranking.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n5) The number of skipped tokens (we use this for infix matches). This is another byte. This is used for reranking, to give priority to prefix queries (skipped tokens = 0) over infix queries, and if all the matches are infix, to give the ones where the matched word is closer to the beginning of the sentence).\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe sentences are quite repetitive, but we don\'t seem to achieve an optimal compression. A GZ-compressed file of 250MB is generating a FST of around 1.9GB. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eWe\'ve applied the patch to trunk, but I cannot get it to compile. Maybe the version that is uploaded to JIRA is out of date. Do you have a newer version?\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThanks a lot,\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nCarlos\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13162156_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=gonzalezcarlos2\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Carlos Gonz\\u00E1lez-Cadenas\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13162156_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'03\\/Dec\\/11 15:31\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-12-03T15:31:51+0000\'\u003e03\\/Dec\\/11 15:31\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    Hello Dawid: \\n\\n First of all, for the FSTLookup we\'re using a FST and not a FSA, that means that we\'ve replaced the NoOutputs with ByteSequenceOutputs. The reason for this is that our autocomplete system requires to get some metadata about the sentence being matched, because we do some post-match reranking of the results in order to get quality suggestions (the buckets themselves are quite big and the results are quite poor without reranking, specially for short prefixes) \\n\\n The queries we use with the FSTLookup are generated using templates. Our domain is hotels, simplifying things that means that we have K templates (i.e. an example template could be hotels + amenity + city), then we have I individuals (i.e. all the cities in the world ), and we generate queries like: \\n\\n hotels with jacuzzi in barcelona \\n\\n The output for this key contains some metadata that is useful for reranking matches or displaying the matches to the user. We encode it in as few bytes as possible, and we make sure that things that are common to many sentences are put first so that they can get compacted appropriately. The metadata in the output is the following (in order): \\n\\n 1) Display version of the sentence. The match sentence described above is normalized and transliterated to ASCII, i.e. it converts acutes to normal characters, and stuff like this. We have the \\\"display\\\" version to show the correctly formatted version to the user. We apply simple transliteration rules so that the differnece between the display and the match is not very big (i.e. , we don\'t apply stuff like pinyin transliteration for chinese). \\n2) The ID of the city (an int that will help us to later execute the query and give the right results) \\n3) The \\\"score\\\" of the sentence (float, used to rerank the matches) \\n4) A byte to represent the number of alternate names used in the query (i.e. \\\"barcelona\\\" is also referred as \\\"la ciudad condal\\\", if the prefix is \\\"hotels in\\\" we don\'t want to produce both matches, just the most common one. This value is used for reranking. \\n5) The number of skipped tokens (we use this for infix matches). This is another byte. This is used for reranking, to give priority to prefix queries (skipped tokens = 0) over infix queries, and if all the matches are infix, to give the ones where the matched word is closer to the beginning of the sentence). \\n\\n The sentences are quite repetitive, but we don\'t seem to achieve an optimal compression. A GZ-compressed file of 250MB is generating a FST of around 1.9GB.  \\n\\n We\'ve applied the patch to trunk, but I cannot get it to compile. Maybe the version that is uploaded to JIRA is out of date. James, do you have a version of this patch that works with trunk? \\n\\n Thanks a lot.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-13162719\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/LUCENE-3298?focusedCommentId=13162719&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-13162719\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"dweiss\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13162719_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=dweiss\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"dweiss\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Dawid Weiss\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  -              \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-13162752\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/LUCENE-3298?focusedCommentId=13162752&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-13162752\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13162752_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=gonzalezcarlos2\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Carlos Gonz\\u00E1lez-Cadenas\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13162752_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'05\\/Dec\\/11 12:45\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-12-05T12:45:55+0000\'\u003e05\\/Dec\\/11 12:45\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eYeap, at the beginning of this project we tried to implement this autocomplete system using regular inverted indexes, but the response time required for autocomplete to work from a user perspective is very low (&lt;50ms), and it would be quite hard to achieve such a performance with inverted indexes. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI still think this is the way to go, but as you say we have to be careful with the data generation part. Most of the work should be put in making sure that the data is well distributed and organized in order to avoid combinatorial explosion.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eLet me go in detail with the sources of data permutations and the reasoning behind them:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e1) With regards to infix matches, if a user types \\\"barcelona\\\" we want to match \\\"hotels in barcelona\\\". In order to achieve this, we generate:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ehotels in barcelona =&gt; hotels in barcelona\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nin barcelona =&gt; hotels in barcelona\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nbarcelona =&gt; hotels in barcelona\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe FST should be able to conflate these prefixes nicely in just one path, right?. Therefore this part shouldn\'t be a problem.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e2) In addition, another feature we want to achieve is to be able to match inputs without prepositions. That means that if the user types \\\"hotels barcelona jacuzzi\\\", we should be able to match \\\"hoteles in barcelona with jacuzzi\\\". Now the only way we envision of doing it properly is to generate this permutation within the data:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ehotels barcelona jacuzzi =&gt; hotels in barcelona with jacuzzi\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI can see how this can explode the FST by creating different branches. Theoretically this could be done at runtime without the need of generating the data, but we don\'t see a way to do it in a clean way. To make things more complicated \u003cimg class=\\\"emoticon\\\" src=\\\"\\/jira\\/images\\/icons\\/emoticons\\/smile.png\\\" height=\\\"16\\\" width=\\\"16\\\" align=\\\"absmiddle\\\" alt=\\\"\\\" border=\\\"0\\\"\\/\u003e we\'ve implemented fuzzy matching at query time (we use a levenshtein automata generated with the user input + an edit distance and then we intersect with the FST), and this is making very complicated to do preposition handling at query time. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e3) PP permutations (i.e. hoteles in barcelona with jacuzzi and hoteles with jacuzzi in barcelona). I don\'t really see a way to work around this. Probably we need to be careful and only generate these permutations for the top-K cities, in order to limit the potential size.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eSummarizing, I believe that we can reduce the set of \\\"bad permutations\\\" a lot if we can figure out how to implement the prepositions at runtime. If you have any ideas, let me know. Thanks! \u003cimg class=\\\"emoticon\\\" src=\\\"\\/jira\\/images\\/icons\\/emoticons\\/smile.png\\\" height=\\\"16\\\" width=\\\"16\\\" align=\\\"absmiddle\\\" alt=\\\"\\\" border=\\\"0\\\"\\/\u003e\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13162752_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=gonzalezcarlos2\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Carlos Gonz\\u00E1lez-Cadenas\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13162752_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'05\\/Dec\\/11 12:45\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-12-05T12:45:55+0000\'\u003e05\\/Dec\\/11 12:45\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    Yeap, at the beginning of this project we tried to implement this autocomplete system using regular inverted indexes, but the response time required for autocomplete to work from a user perspective is very low (&lt;50ms), and it would be quite hard to achieve such a performance with inverted indexes.  \\n\\n I still think this is the way to go, but as you say we have to be careful with the data generation part. Most of the work should be put in making sure that the data is well distributed and organized in order to avoid combinatorial explosion. \\n\\n Let me go in detail with the sources of data permutations and the reasoning behind them: \\n\\n 1) With regards to infix matches, if a user types \\\"barcelona\\\" we want to match \\\"hotels in barcelona\\\". In order to achieve this, we generate: \\n\\n hotels in barcelona =&gt; hotels in barcelona \\nin barcelona =&gt; hotels in barcelona \\nbarcelona =&gt; hotels in barcelona \\n\\n The FST should be able to conflate these prefixes nicely in just one path, right?. Therefore this part shouldn\'t be a problem. \\n\\n 2) In addition, another feature we want to achieve is to be able to match inputs without prepositions. That means that if the user types \\\"hotels barcelona jacuzzi\\\", we should be able to match \\\"hoteles in barcelona with jacuzzi\\\". Now the only way we envision of doing it properly is to generate this permutation within the data: \\n\\n hotels barcelona jacuzzi =&gt; hotels in barcelona with jacuzzi \\n\\n I can see how this can explode the FST by creating different branches. Theoretically this could be done at runtime without the need of generating the data, but we don\'t see a way to do it in a clean way. To make things more complicated   we\'ve implemented fuzzy matching at query time (we use a levenshtein automata generated with the user input + an edit distance and then we intersect with the FST), and this is making very complicated to do preposition handling at query time.  \\n\\n 3) PP permutations (i.e. hoteles in barcelona with jacuzzi and hoteles with jacuzzi in barcelona). I don\'t really see a way to work around this. Probably we need to be careful and only generate these permutations for the top-K cities, in order to limit the potential size. \\n\\n Summarizing, I believe that we can reduce the set of \\\"bad permutations\\\" a lot if we can figure out how to implement the prepositions at runtime. If you have any ideas, let me know. Thanks!   \\n\\n             \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-13163425\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/LUCENE-3298?focusedCommentId=13163425&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-13163425\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"dweiss\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13163425_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=dweiss\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"dweiss\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Dawid Weiss\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13163425_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'06\\/Dec\\/11 08:14\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-12-06T08:14:52+0000\'\u003e06\\/Dec\\/11 08:14\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cblockquote\u003e\u003cp\u003etime required for autocomplete to work from a user perspective is very low (&lt;50ms),\u003c\\/p\u003e\u003c\\/blockquote\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI\'ve seen a presentation by Greg Donovan at Lucene Revolution San Francisco, here:\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\u003ca href=\\\"http:\\/\\/www.lucidimagination.com\\/devzone\\/events\\/conferences\\/revolution\\/2011\\/solr-and-lucene-etsy\\\" class=\\\"external-link\\\" rel=\\\"nofollow\\\"\u003ehttp:\\/\\/www.lucidimagination.com\\/devzone\\/events\\/conferences\\/revolution\\/2011\\/solr-and-lucene-etsy\u003c\\/a\u003e\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ethey seem to have a lot of traffic and still use a shard of Solr servers to do contextual suggestions. Maybe it\'d be easier to buy more hardware than try to squeeze something into an FST that it doesn\'t handle well (permutations). Just a thought.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\u003cp\u003ehotels in barcelona =&gt; hotels in barcelona, The FST should be able to conflate these prefixes nicely in just one path, right?.\u003c\\/p\u003e\u003c\\/blockquote\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe FST will be able to conflate suffixes if you have no outputs. If you do have different outputs these need to be stored somewhere too; for outputs with a common part, the common part is pushed towards the root of the FST, but for byte sequences this is unlikely so the output will actually have to differentiate these paths somehow and create at least a single separate node\\/arc in the FST. I tell this without checking, but this is my intuition &#8211; verify in practice if you want to.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"dweiss\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13163425_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=dweiss\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"dweiss\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Dawid Weiss\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13163425_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'06\\/Dec\\/11 08:14\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-12-06T08:14:52+0000\'\u003e06\\/Dec\\/11 08:14\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                     time required for autocomplete to work from a user perspective is very low (&lt;50ms),  \\n\\n I\'ve seen a presentation by Greg Donovan at Lucene Revolution San Francisco, here: \\n http:\\/\\/www.lucidimagination.com\\/devzone\\/events\\/conferences\\/revolution\\/2011\\/solr-and-lucene-etsy  \\n\\n they seem to have a lot of traffic and still use a shard of Solr servers to do contextual suggestions. Just a thought. \\n\\n  hotels in barcelona =&gt; hotels in barcelona, The FST should be able to conflate these prefixes nicely in just one path, right?.  \\n\\n The FST will be able to conflate suffixes if you have no outputs.   \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eHi Sudarshan,\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI don\'t believe that my implementation is gonna be of much practical value for the general public. Note that, as described above, in my implementation I store custom data that is useful for my application, but it almost certainly won\'t make any sense for the rest of applications.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI\'m happy to tell you how to modify the code to store your own outputs, it\'s quite easy: \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n1) First you have to enable it at the code level, you just need to change NoOutputs by ByteSequenceOutputs and then in all the references of Arc&lt;Object&gt; or FST&lt;Object&gt; you need to change them by Arc&lt;BytesRef&gt; and FST&lt;BytesRef&gt;. \u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n2) At build time, you need to store something in the output. You can do it by creating the appropriate BytesRef and including it in the builder.add() call instead of the placeholder value that is present now.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n3) At query time, you need to collect the output while traversing the FST (note that the output may be scattered through the whole arc chain) and then you can process it in the way specific to your app. Probably you want to do it in the collect() method (when the LookupResults are created).\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI believe that\'s all. If you have any questions, let me know.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThanks\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nCarlos\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13164632_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=gonzalezcarlos2\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"gonzalezcarlos2\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Carlos Gonz\\u00E1lez-Cadenas\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13164632_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'07\\/Dec\\/11 19:21\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-12-07T19:21:11+0000\'\u003e07\\/Dec\\/11 19:21\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    Hi Sudarshan, \\n\\n I don\'t believe that my implementation is gonna be of much practical value for the general public. Note that, as described above, in my implementation I store custom data that is useful for my application, but it almost certainly won\'t make any sense for the rest of applications. \\n\\n I\'m happy to tell you how to modify the code to store your own outputs, it\'s quite easy:  \\n1) First you have to enable it at the code level, you just need to change NoOutputs by ByteSequenceOutputs and then in all the references of Arc&lt;Object&gt; or FST&lt;Object&gt; you need to change them by Arc&lt;BytesRef&gt; and FST&lt;BytesRef&gt;.  \\n2) At build time, you need to store something in the output. You can do it by creating the appropriate BytesRef and including it in the builder.add() call instead of the placeholder value that is present now. \\n3) At query time, you need to collect the output while traversing the FST (note that the output may be scattered through the whole arc chain) and then you can process it in the way specific to your app. Probably you want to do it in the collect() method (when the LookupResults are created). \\n\\n I believe that\'s all.
